return null}

<script>document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",function(){const lightboxHTML=`
        <div id="simple-lightbox">
            <span class="lb-close">&times;</span>
            <div class="lb-nav lb-prev">&#8249;</div> <div class="lb-nav lb-next">&#8250;</div>
            <img id="lightbox-img" src="" alt="Zoomed Image">
            <div id="lightbox-caption" class="lb-caption-text"></div>
        </div>
    `;document.body.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend',lightboxHTML);const lightbox=document.getElementById('simple-lightbox');const lightboxImg=document.getElementById('lightbox-img');const lightboxCap=document.getElementById('lightbox-caption');const lbPrev=document.querySelector('.lb-prev');const lbNext=document.querySelector('.lb-next');let currentGalleryData=[];let currentIndex=0;const galleries=document.querySelectorAll('.wp-block-gallery.has-nested-images');galleries.forEach((gallery)=>{const wrapper=document.createElement('div');wrapper.className='gallery-slider-wrapper';gallery.parentNode.insertBefore(wrapper,gallery);wrapper.appendChild(gallery);const btnPrev=document.createElement('div');btnPrev.className='slider-arrow prev';btnPrev.innerHTML='&#8249;';const btnNext=document.createElement('div');btnNext.className='slider-arrow next';btnNext.innerHTML='&#8250;';wrapper.appendChild(btnPrev);wrapper.appendChild(btnNext);btnPrev.addEventListener('click',()=>{gallery.scrollBy({left:-450,behavior:'smooth'})});btnNext.addEventListener('click',()=>{gallery.scrollBy({left:450,behavior:'smooth'})});const items=gallery.querySelectorAll('figure.wp-block-image');const localData=Array.from(items).map(item=>{const img=item.querySelector('img');const capEl=item.querySelector('figcaption');const src=img.getAttribute('data-src')||img.src;const text=capEl?capEl.innerText:'';return{src:src,text:text,element:img}});localData.forEach((data,index)=>{data.element.addEventListener('click',(e)=>{e.preventDefault();currentGalleryData=localData;currentIndex=index;openLightbox()})})});function openLightbox(){updateContent();lightbox.classList.add('active')}
function updateContent(){lightboxImg.style.opacity='0.5';lightboxCap.style.opacity='0';setTimeout(()=>{const item=currentGalleryData[currentIndex];lightboxImg.src=item.src;if(item.text&&item.text.trim()!==""){lightboxCap.innerText=item.text;lightboxCap.style.display="block"}else{lightboxCap.style.display="none"}
lightboxImg.style.opacity='1';lightboxCap.style.opacity='1'},150)}
function nextImage(){currentIndex++;if(currentIndex>=currentGalleryData.length)currentIndex=0;updateContent()}
function prevImage(){currentIndex--;if(currentIndex<0)currentIndex=currentGalleryData.length-1;updateContent()}
lbNext.addEventListener('click',(e)=>{e.stopPropagation();nextImage()});lbPrev.addEventListener('click',(e)=>{e.stopPropagation();prevImage()});let touchStartX=0;let touchEndX=0;lightbox.addEventListener('touchstart',(e)=>touchStartX=e.changedTouches[0].screenX,{passive:!0});lightbox.addEventListener('touchend',(e)=>{touchEndX=e.changedTouches[0].screenX;if(touchEndX<touchStartX-50)nextImage();if(touchEndX>touchStartX+50)prevImage();},{passive:!0});const closeBtn=document.querySelector('.lb-close');function closeLightbox(){lightbox.classList.remove('active');lightboxImg.src=''}
closeBtn.addEventListener('click',closeLightbox);lightbox.addEventListener('click',(e)=>{if(e.target===lightbox||e.target.id==='simple-lightbox')closeLightbox();});document.addEventListener('keydown',(e)=>{if(e.key==="Escape")closeLightbox();if(e.key==="ArrowRight"&&lightbox.classList.contains('active'))nextImage();if(e.key==="ArrowLeft"&&lightbox.classList.contains('active'))prevImage();})})</script> </body></html>
